                            Longitude 58°09′W. (Middle Arm Point), thence to Latitude
                            49°11′N., Longitude 58°07′W. (North Arm Point), and thence
                            to Latitude 49°14′N., Longitude 58°12′W. (Crab Point).
                23.         In that portion of any river estuary in Nova Scotia, New        Gill nets         Jan. 1 to Dec. 31
                            Brunswick or Prince Edward Island that is upstream of the
                            first point where that estuary is 0.8 km in width at normal low
                            tide.
